$output(opts) =>
  delete window.EditContext; // <-- until this is fixed: https://issues.chromium.org/issues/371791303
  
  if(!window.textEditorPluginMeta9973752983) {
    window.textEditorPluginMeta9973752983 = {
      codemirror6: getCodemirror6Imports(),
    };
  }
  
  const { CMState, CMView, CMCommands, CMLanguage, CMSearch, yjs, lezerHighlightTags, oneDark, createInlineCopilotExtension, yCollab } = window.textEditorPluginMeta9973752983.codemirror6;
  
  let { EditorView, placeholder, MatchDecorator, ViewPlugin, Decoration, highlightActiveLineGutter, highlightSpecialChars, drawSelection, dropCursor, rectangularSelection, crosshairCursor, highlightActiveLine, keymap } = CMView;
  let { EditorState, Compartment, EditorSelection, Text } = CMState;
  let { indentWithTab, history, defaultKeymap, historyKeymap } = CMCommands;
  let { indentUnit, syntaxHighlighting, HighlightStyle } = CMLanguage;
  let { searchKeymap, highlightSelectionMatches } = CMSearch;
  
  let darkTheme = oneDark;
  let lightTheme = [];
  
  const spellcheckCompartment = new Compartment();
  let currentSpellcheckBoolean = true;
  const placeholderCompartment = new Compartment();
  let currentPlaceholderText = "";
  
  function createEditorState(opts={}) {
    let extensions = [
      history(),
      drawSelection(),
      indentUnit.of("  "),
      EditorState.tabSize.of(2),
      EditorState.allowMultipleSelections.of(true),
      dropCursor(),
      // crosshairCursor(),
      // highlightSelectionMatches(),
      // yCollab(opts.yText),
      // createInlineCopilotExtension(opts.docId),
      spellcheckCompartment.of(EditorView.contentAttributes.of({ spellcheck: currentSpellcheckBoolean ? true : false })),
      EditorView.contentAttributes.of({autocapitalize:"on"}),
      placeholderCompartment.of(placeholder(currentPlaceholderText)),
      EditorView.lineWrapping,
      keymap.of([
        // indentWithTab, // CAUTION: commented out because this must be an opt-in feature, else it messes with e.g. ai-story-generator tab to autocomplete
        ...defaultKeymap,
        ...searchKeymap,
        ...historyKeymap,
      ]),
      // syntaxHighlighting(HighlightStyle.define([
      //   {tag: lezerHighlightTags.variableName, color: "light-dark(#c50074, #e66556)"},
      //   {tag: lezerHighlightTags.definition(lezerHighlightTags.variableName), color: "light-dark(#c67600, #e5c07b)"},
      //   {tag: lezerHighlightTags.local(lezerHighlightTags.variableName), color: "light-dark(#268BD2, #cacaca)"},
      //   {tag: lezerHighlightTags.propertyName, color: "light-dark(#435156, #56b6c2)"},
      //   {tag: lezerHighlightTags.typeOperator, color: "light-dark(#CB4B16, #fcae1d)"},
      // ])),
      EditorView.theme({}, { dark: opts.darkMode }),
      EditorView.baseTheme({
        '&': { textAlign:"left", fontFamily:"inherit", display:"inline-flex !important", width:"100%", height:"100%", },
        ".cm-scroller": {fontFamily: "inherit"},
      }),
    ];
  
    if(opts.darkMode !== false && window.matchMedia && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches) {
      extensions.push(opts.themeCompartment.of(darkTheme));
    } else {
      extensions.push(opts.themeCompartment.of(lightTheme));
    }
    
    if(opts.extensions) extensions.push(...opts.extensions);
  
    // return EditorState.create({ doc:opts.yText.toString() || "", extensions });
    return EditorState.create({ doc:"", extensions });
  }
  
  function createTextEditor(opts={}) {
    // let docId = opts.docId ?? Math.random().toString(36).substring(7);
    // let yDoc = opts.yDoc;
    // if(!yDoc && !opts.yText) yDoc = new yjs.Doc();
    // let yText = opts.yText ?? yDoc.getText(docId);
    // if(opts.value !== undefined) yText.insert(0, opts.value.toString());

    let element = document.createElement("div");
    
    let editorView;
    
    let eventHandlers = {}; // eventName => [handlerFn1, handlerFn2, ...]

    // document.addEventListener("selectionchange", function() {
    //   if(editorView.dom.contains(document.activeElement)) {
    //     eventHandlers["selectionchange"].forEach(h => { try { h({}); } catch(e) { console.error(e); } });
    //   }
    // });
    
    // function waitForSubtreeToBeMutated(el) {
    //   let resolver; // must add observer synchronously so we don't miss a mutation
    //   let observer = new MutationObserver(_ => {
    //     resolver();
    //     observer.disconnect();
    //   }); 
    //   observer.observe(el, { childList:true, attributes:true });
    //   return new Promise(r => resolver=r);
    // }
    
    const docChangeListener = ViewPlugin.fromClass(class {
      update(update) {
        if(update.selectionSet) {
          if(eventHandlers["selectionchange"]) {
            setTimeout(() => { // TODO: Does Codemirror6 have a way to force-render the cursor/highlights?
              eventHandlers["selectionchange"].forEach(h => { try { h({}); } catch(e) { console.error(e); } });
            }, 15); // Hacky, but it'll do for now. It's needed to wait for Codemirror's selection elements to move/be created (based on testing, it seems like it has a delay/debounce of 10ms)
          }
        }
        if(update.docChanged) {
          // console.log("UPDATE:", update);

          // EDIT: Lines below are commented out because THIS IS WRONG!
          // Because change/input only fires on *user* typed/pasted/etc. input, but this change listener fires on ANY changes to the doc.
          // if(eventHandlers["change"]) eventHandlers["change"].forEach(h => { try { h({}); } catch(e) { queueMicrotask(() => { throw e; }); } });
          // if(eventHandlers["input"]) eventHandlers["input"].forEach(h => { try { h({}); } catch(e) { queueMicrotask(() => { throw e; }); } });
          // if(element.onchange) { try { element.onchange({}); } catch(e) { queueMicrotask(() => { throw e; }); } }
          // if(element.oninput) { try { element.oninput({}); } catch(e) { queueMicrotask(() => { throw e; }); } }
        }
      }
    });

    // if(opts.onInput) eventHandlers.input = [opts.onInput];
    // else if(opts.oninput) eventHandlers.input = [opts.oninput];
    // if(opts.onChange) eventHandlers.change = [opts.onChange];
    // else if(opts.onchange) eventHandlers.change = [opts.onchange];
  
    let themeCompartment = new Compartment();
    let textStyleCompartment = new Compartment();

    function buildTextStyleExtensions(rules) {
      let textStyleDecorations = rules || [];
      let textStyleExtensions = [];
      for(let {match, style} of textStyleDecorations) {
        const decorator = new MatchDecorator({
          regexp: match,
          decoration: Decoration.mark({attributes: {style}})
        });
        const plugin = ViewPlugin.fromClass(class {
          constructor(view) { this.decorations = decorator.createDeco(view); }
          update(update) { this.decorations = decorator.updateDeco(update, this.decorations); }
        }, { decorations: v => v.decorations });
        textStyleExtensions.push(plugin);
      }
      return textStyleExtensions;
    }
    let textStyleExtensions = buildTextStyleExtensions(opts.textStyleRules || []);
    
    let editorState = createEditorState({
      placeholder: opts.placeholder || "",
      // yText,
      // docId,
      themeCompartment,
      extensions: [...(opts.extraStateExtensions ?? []), docChangeListener, textStyleCompartment.of(textStyleExtensions)],
    });
    
    editorView = new EditorView({
      state: editorState,
      parent: null,
    });
    // element = editorView.dom;
    element.append(editorView.dom);
    element.setTextStyleRules = (rules) => {
      element.textStyleRules = rules || [];
      textStyleExtensions = buildTextStyleExtensions(element.textStyleRules);
      editorView.dispatch({effects: textStyleCompartment.reconfigure(textStyleExtensions)});
    };
    element.updateTextStyleRules = element.setTextStyleRules;

    // yText.observe(event => {
    //   cachedText = null;
    // });

    let cachedText = "";

    // NOTE: I checked, and cm6 does *not* do caching internally. This improves perf considerably.
    // Not sure how expensive doc.toString() is so I'm caching it, which means stuff like `for(let i = 0; i < editorEl.value.length; i++) { ... }` is not expensive.
    // To be extremely safe, we wrap the dispatch to ensure cache is always cleared.
    const originalEditorViewDispatch = editorView.dispatch.bind(editorView);
    editorView.dispatch = function(...args) {
      cachedText = null;
      originalEditorViewDispatch(...args); // before this call, the textContent of the cm-editor doesn't have the update, even when user is manually typing in the textarea
    };
    
    const getText = () => {
      // if(cachedText === null) cachedText = yText.toString();
      if(cachedText === null) cachedText = editorView.state.doc.toString();
      return cachedText;
    };

    // yText.observe(event => {
    //   console.log("Changes:", event.changes.delta);
    // });

    let diff = fastDiff_Module().default;

    function efficientlyUpdateEditorContent(editorView, newText, editPos) {
      const currentText = editorView.state.doc.toString();
      const changes = diff(currentText, newText, editPos);
      let changeSpecs = [];
      let pos = 0;
    
      for (const [type, value] of changes) {
        if (type === diff.DELETE) {
          changeSpecs.push({ from: pos, to: pos + value.length });
          pos += value.length;
        } else if (type === diff.INSERT) {
          changeSpecs.push({ from: pos, insert: value });
        } else { // EQUAL
          pos += value.length;
        }
      }
    
      if (changeSpecs.length > 0) {
        editorView.dispatch({ changes: changeSpecs });
      }
    }

    function forceRender() {
      const originalScrollTop = editorView.scrollDOM.scrollTop;
      editorView.scrollDOM.scrollTop += 1;
      editorView.scrollDOM.scrollTop -= 1;
      editorView.scrollDOM.scrollTop = originalScrollTop;
    }

    // a one-time forced render (not 'layout'? idk) is sometimes needed in latest chrome as of writing - weird race condition of some sort i guess
    // let alreadyDoneInitialForceRender = false;
    
    let needsInitialForceRender = false;
    let alreadyDoneInitialForceRender = false;
    let resizeObs = new ResizeObserver(entries => {
      if (!alreadyDoneInitialForceRender && needsInitialForceRender && entries[0].contentRect.height > 0) {
        alreadyDoneInitialForceRender = true;
        editorView.requestMeasure();
        forceRender();
        resizeObs.disconnect();
      }
    });
    resizeObs.observe(element);
    
    const setText = (text) => {
      let current = getText();
      let next = typeof text === "string" ? text : text.toString();
      if(current === next) return;

      // NOTE: this commented-out 'plain' dispatch is actually *faster* BUT produces huge update objects, which causes OOM very quickly if e.g. there's 5mb of text in the editor and you do a few hundred calls to this setText function.
      // editorView.dispatch({changes:{ from:0, to:editorView.state.doc.length, insert:text }});
      let t = performance.now();
      efficientlyUpdateEditorContent(editorView, text);
      console.debug("efficientlyUpdateEditorContent: time taken:", performance.now()-t);
      // if(!alreadyDoneInitialForceRender) { alreadyDoneInitialForceRender = true; setTimeout(forceRender, 0); }
      if(!alreadyDoneInitialForceRender) { needsInitialForceRender = true; }
    };
    
    element.appendText = (text) => { // this is much faster than setText for appending to multi-megabyte texts
      let t = typeof text === "string" ? text : text.toString();
      // yText.insert(yText.length, t);
      editorView.dispatch({changes: {from:editorView.state.doc.length, insert:text}});
      // if(!alreadyDoneInitialForceRender) { alreadyDoneInitialForceRender = true; setTimeout(forceRender, 0); }
      if(!alreadyDoneInitialForceRender) { needsInitialForceRender = true; }
    };
    Object.defineProperty(element, 'spellcheck', {
      get: function() { return currentSpellcheckBoolean; },
      set: function(value) { value = Boolean(value); currentSpellcheckBoolean=value; editorView.dispatch({effects:spellcheckCompartment.reconfigure(EditorView.contentAttributes.of({ spellcheck: currentSpellcheckBoolean ? true : false }))}); return value; }
    });
    Object.defineProperty(element, 'placeholder', {
      get: function() { return currentPlaceholderText; },
      set: function(value) { value = value.toString(); currentPlaceholderText=value; editorView.dispatch({effects:placeholderCompartment.reconfigure(placeholder(value))}); return value; }
    });
    Object.defineProperty(element, 'value', {
      get: function() { return getText(); },
      set: function(value) { return setText(value); }
    });

    function maybeForceEditorLayout() {
      // coordsAtPos hackily triggers synchronous layout, which is neccessary for accurate values if text has just been set/edited
      // need to try/catch because it throws if it's called during an cm6 'update' (no idea)
      let t = performance.now();
      try { editorView.coordsAtPos(1); } catch(e) {} // TODO: see why this throws "Reading the editor layout isn't allowed during an update" sometimes
      let timeTaken = performance.now()-t;
      if(timeTaken > 5) console.warn("text-editor-plugin-v1: maybeForceEditorLayout: time taken:", timeTaken);
    }
    
    Object.defineProperty(element, 'scrollTop', {
      get: function() { maybeForceEditorLayout(); return editorView.scrollDOM.scrollTop; },
      set: function(value) { maybeForceEditorLayout(); return editorView.scrollDOM.scrollTop=value; },
    });

    // NOTE: This unfortunately gets called internally by codemirror during some sort scroll handling, since it climbs up the tree to <body>, which may confuse it.
    // Haven't found any issues yet though. Not sure why it's climbing up to <body> and checking scroll heights.
    Object.defineProperty(element, 'scrollHeight', {
      get: function() { maybeForceEditorLayout(); return editorView.scrollDOM.scrollHeight; },
    });

    element.focus = function(...args) { editorView.focus(); }; // returning undefined is correct behavior

    // Proxy a bunch of methods to scrollDOM, since that's the element we're treating as the 'actual' editor:
    for(let method of ["querySelector", "querySelectorAll", "append", "appendChild", "prepend"]) {
      element[method] = editorView.scrollDOM[method].bind(editorView.scrollDOM);
    }

    // This is a non-<textarea> property that gives relative and absolute details about the position of the caret with respect to this editor, and relative to the viewport.
    // document.querySelector(".cm-layer.cm-selectionLayer .cm-selectionBackground") // <-- this effectively gives us the position of the selectionStart, assuming that selectionStart!==selectionEnd, but note that it's an ephemeral element, and there is one of them per line in the selection. (whereas there is only one cm-cursor-primary and it always exists [just sometimes hidden])
    // TODO: consider just adding an element.selectionAnchor property or something, which allows you to position elements relative to the selection, via a few config options.
    let caretCtn = editorView.dom.querySelector(".cm-layer.cm-layer-above.cm-cursorLayer");
    let cachedCaretObservation = {isVisible:false, offsetLeft:0, offsetTop:0, offsetWidth:0, offsetHeight:0};
    let caretObserveCallbacks = [];
    function addCaretObservers() {
      function getObservation() {
        let caretCoords = editorView.coordsAtPos(editorView.state.selection.main.head, editorView.state.selection.main.assoc);
        let scrollDOM = editorView.scrollDOM;
        let scrollDOMRect = scrollDOM.getBoundingClientRect();

        // hacky, but it'll do for now:
        let caretHeight = Number(getComputedStyle(scrollDOM.querySelector(".cm-line")).fontSize.replace("px", ""))*1.13;

        const isVisible = document.hasFocus() && scrollDOM.contains(document.activeElement);
        return {
          isVisible,
          offsetLeft: isVisible ? caretCoords.left - scrollDOMRect.left + scrollDOM.scrollLeft : 0,
          offsetTop: isVisible ? caretCoords.top - scrollDOMRect.top + scrollDOM.scrollTop : 0,
          offsetWidth: isVisible ? 1 : 0,
          offsetHeight: isVisible ? caretHeight : 0,
        };
        
        // OLD APPROACH (can't use because CM6 doesn't add a cursor element for iOS Safari, since native one can't be hidden):
        // let caretEl = editorView.dom.querySelector(".cm-cursor.cm-cursor-primary");
        // return {
        //   isVisible: (caretEl?.offsetHeight !== 0) ?? false,
        //   offsetLeft: caretEl?.offsetLeft ?? 0,
        //   offsetTop: caretEl?.offsetTop ?? 0,
        //   offsetWidth: caretEl?.offsetWidth ?? 0,
        //   offsetHeight: caretEl?.offsetHeight ?? 0,
        // };
      };

      function runCaretObserverCallbacks() {
        let errors = [];
        for(let c of caretObserveCallbacks) {
          try { c(getObservation()) } catch(e) { queueMicrotask(() => { throw e; }); }
        }
      }
      
      let caretMutationObserver = new MutationObserver(mutations => { 
        if(mutations.some(m => m.attributeName === "style")) {
          runCaretObserverCallbacks();
          cachedCaretObservation = getObservation();
        }
      });
      caretMutationObserver.observe(caretCtn, { attributes: true, attributeFilter: ['style', 'top', 'left'] });
      
      let lastKnownVisibility = undefined;
      let caretResizeObserver = new ResizeObserver(entries => {
        for (const entry of entries) {
          let visible = entry.contentRect.height !== 0;
          if(visible !== lastKnownVisibility) {
            lastKnownVisibility = visible;
            runCaretObserverCallbacks();
          }
        }
      });
      caretResizeObserver.observe(caretCtn);
    }
    if(caretCtn) {
      addCaretObservers();
    } else {
      let observer = new MutationObserver(mutations => { 
        caretCtn = editorView.dom.querySelector(".cm-layer.cm-layer-above.cm-cursorLayer");
        if(caretCtn) {
          addCaretObservers();
          observer.disconnect();
        }
      });
      observer.observe(editorView.scrollDOM, { childList:true });
    }
    
    Object.defineProperty(element, 'caret', {
      value: {
        // get element() { return caretEl; }, // (EDIT: iOS safari doesn't have an element for caret in CM6) necessary e.g. for CSS anchoring API
        get isVisible() { return cachedCaretObservation.isVisible; },
        get offsetLeft() { return cachedCaretObservation.offsetLeft; },
        get offsetTop() { return cachedCaretObservation.offsetTop; },
        get offsetWidth() { return cachedCaretObservation.offsetWidth; },
        get offsetHeight() { return cachedCaretObservation.offsetHeight; },
        observe(cb) {
          caretObserveCallbacks.push(cb);
        },
        unobserve(cb) {
          caretObserveCallbacks = caretObserveCallbacks.filter(c => c !== cb);
        },
      },
    });

    // necessary e.g. for CSS anchoring API:
    let selectionBackgroundCtn = document.querySelector(".cm-layer.cm-selectionLayer");
    let getSelectionEls = () => {
      if(!selectionBackgroundCtn) selectionBackgroundCtn = document.querySelector(".cm-layer.cm-selectionLayer");
      return selectionBackgroundCtn.querySelectorAll(".cm-selectionBackground");
    }
    Object.defineProperty(element, 'selectionLayout', {
      value: {
        start: {
          get offsetTop() {
            let els = getSelectionEls();
            if(els.length === 0) return cachedCaretObservation.offsetTop;
            return els[0].offsetTop;
          },
          get offsetLeft() {
            let els = getSelectionEls();
            if(els.length === 0) return cachedCaretObservation.offsetLeft;
            return els[0].offsetLeft;
          },
          get offsetHeight() {
            let els = getSelectionEls();
            if(els.length === 0) return cachedCaretObservation.offsetHeight;
            return els[0].offsetHeight;
          },
        },
        end: {
          get offsetTop() {
            let els = getSelectionEls();
            if(els.length === 0) return cachedCaretObservation.offsetTop;
            if(els.length === 1) return els[0].offsetTop;
            if(els.length === 2) return els[1].offsetTop;
            if(els.length === 3) return els[2].offsetTop;
          },
          get offsetLeft() {
            let els = getSelectionEls();
            if(els.length === 0) return cachedCaretObservation.offsetLeft;
            if(els.length === 1) return els[0].offsetLeft + els[0].offsetWidth;
            if(els.length === 2) return els[1].offsetLeft + els[1].offsetWidth;
            if(els.length === 3) return els[2].offsetLeft + els[2].offsetWidth;
          },
          get offsetHeight() {
            let els = getSelectionEls();
            if(els.length === 0) return cachedCaretObservation.offsetHeight;
            return els[0].offsetHeight; // (line height height will always be the same as the first line)
          },
        },
      },
    });
    
    Object.defineProperty(element, 'selectionStart', {
      get: function() { return editorView.state.selection.main.from; },
      set: function(value) {
        let start = value;
        let end = editorView.state.selection.main.to;
        if(end < start) end = start; // push end forward to newly specified start (to match <textarea> behavior)
        editorView.dispatch({ selection: EditorSelection.single(start, end) });
        return value;
      },
    });
    Object.defineProperty(element, 'selectionEnd', {
      get: function() { return editorView.state.selection.main.to; },
      set: function(value) {
        let start = editorView.state.selection.main.from;
        let end = value;
        if(start > end) start = end; // push start back to newly-specified end (to match <textarea> behavior)
        editorView.dispatch({ selection: EditorSelection.single(start, end) });
        return value;
      },
    });

    // Make blur and focus work by using bubbling versions:
    element.addEventListener("focusout", function() {
      if(eventHandlers["blur"]) eventHandlers["blur"].forEach(h => { try { h({}); } catch(e) { queueMicrotask(() => { throw e; }); } });
      if(element.onblur) { try { element.onblur({}); } catch(e) { queueMicrotask(() => { throw e; }); } }
    });
    element.addEventListener("focusin", function() {
      if(eventHandlers["focus"]) eventHandlers["focus"].forEach(h => { try { h({}); } catch(e) { queueMicrotask(() => { throw e; }); } });
      if(element.onfocus) { try { element.onfocus({}); } catch(e) { queueMicrotask(() => { throw e; }); } }
    });

    // Create a fake 'onchange', which contenteditable don't have:
    let shouldFireChangeEventOnFocusOut = false;
    element.addEventListener("input", function() {
      shouldFireChangeEventOnFocusOut = true;
    });
    element.addEventListener("focusout", function() {
      if(shouldFireChangeEventOnFocusOut) {
        shouldFireChangeEventOnFocusOut = false;
        if(eventHandlers["change"]) eventHandlers["change"].forEach(h => { try { h({}); } catch(e) { queueMicrotask(() => { throw e; }); } });
        if(element.onchange) { try { element.onchange({}); } catch(e) { queueMicrotask(() => { throw e; }); } }
      }
    });

    // TODO: 'change' event should only fire when the editor `blur`s
    let originalAddEventListener = element.addEventListener.bind(element);
    let originalRemoveEventListener = element.removeEventListener.bind(element);
    element.addEventListener = function(event, handler, opts={}) {
      event = event.toLowerCase();
      if(["change", "selectionchange", "blur", "focus"].includes(event)) {
        let handlerFinal = handler;
        if(opts.once) handlerFinal = (e) => { handler(e); element.removeEventListener(event, handler); };
        if(!eventHandlers[event]) eventHandlers[event] = [];
        eventHandlers[event].push(handlerFinal);
      } else {
        originalAddEventListener(event, handler, opts);
      }
    };
    element.removeEventListener = function(event, handler) {
      event = event.toLowerCase();
      if(["input", "change", "selectionchange", "blur", "focus"].includes(event)) {
        if(!eventHandlers[event]) return;
        eventHandlers[event] = eventHandlers[event].filter(h => h !== handler);
      } else {
        originalRemoveEventListener(event, handler);
      }
    };

    let uniqueId = "a"+Math.random().toString().replace(".", "");

    element.setAttribute(`data-text-editor-v1-${uniqueId}-plugin-styles`, "1");

    // Hacky, but the non-hacky way is more complicated than you'd expect due to the color not just being affected by `prefers-color-scheme: dark`, but also whether any ancestor element has `color-scheme:light dark`.
    // This doesn't handle color-scheme on anything but the html or body, but that's fine for now
    function getCurrentTextareaBackgroundColors() {
      let ctn = document.createElement("div");
      let ta = document.createElement("textarea");
      ctn.append(ta);
      document.body.append(ctn);
      ctn.style.colorScheme = "light";
      let light = getComputedStyle(ta)["background-color"];
      ctn.style.colorScheme = "dark";
      let dark = getComputedStyle(ta)["background-color"];
      ctn.remove();
      if(dark === "rgb(18, 18, 18)") dark = "rgb(59, 59, 59)"; // hacky chrome bug fix
      return {dark, light};
    }
    let textareaBgColors = getCurrentTextareaBackgroundColors();
    
    let defaultStylesElement = document.createElement("style"); 
    document.head.append(defaultStylesElement);
    function updateStyles() {
      let isDarkMode = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
      document.querySelector(':root').style.setProperty(`--text-editor-plugin-v1-${uniqueId}-background-color`, isDarkMode ? textareaBgColors.dark : textareaBgColors.light); // window.getComputedStyle(editorView.dom).backgroundColor);
      
      let textColor = getComputedStyle(element).color;
      document.querySelector(':root').style.setProperty(`--text-editor-plugin-v1-${uniqueId}-caret-color`, textColor);
      
      let paddingStyles = element.style.cssText.split(";").map(r => r.trim()).filter(r => r.startsWith("padding"));
      let paddingLeft = null;
      let paddingRight = null;
      let paddingTop = null;
      let paddingBottom = null;
      for(let style of paddingStyles) {
        let name = style.split(":")[0].trim();
        let value = style.split(":").slice(1).join(":").trim();
        let parts = value.split(/\s+/);
        if(name === "padding") {
          if(parts.length === 1) { paddingTop=paddingRight=paddingBottom=paddingLeft=parts[0]; }
          if(parts.length === 2) { paddingTop=paddingBottom=parts[0]; paddingLeft=paddingRight=parts[1]; }
          if(parts.length === 4) { paddingTop=parts[0]; paddingRight=parts[1]; paddingBottom=parts[2]; paddingLeft=parts[3]; }
        }
        if(name === "padding-top") paddingTop=parts[0];
        if(name === "padding-right") paddingRight=parts[0];
        if(name === "padding-bottom") paddingBottom=parts[0];
        if(name === "padding-left") paddingLeft=parts[0];
      }
      
      defaultStylesElement.textContent = `[data-text-editor-v1-${uniqueId}-plugin-styles='1'] {
        background-color: var(--text-editor-plugin-v1-${uniqueId}-plugin-color);
        background-color: light-dark(${textareaBgColors.light}, ${textareaBgColors.dark});
        border: 1px solid rgba(150, 150, 150, 0.6);
        border-radius: 2px;
        resize:both;
        overflow:hidden;
        display:inline-block;
        padding: 0px !important;
        padding-left: 0px !important;
        padding-right: 0px !important;
        padding-top: 0px !important;
        padding-bottom: 0px !important;
        width: 182px;
        height: 37px;
      }
      [data-text-editor-v1-${uniqueId}-plugin-styles='1'] .cm-cursor {
        border-left-color: var(--text-editor-plugin-v1-${uniqueId}-caret-color) !important;
      }
      [data-text-editor-v1-${uniqueId}-plugin-styles='1']:focus-within {
        outline-offset: -1px;
        outline: 2px solid light-dark(#444, #bbb);
      }
      [data-text-editor-v1-${uniqueId}-plugin-styles='1']:hover {
        border: 1px solid rgba(150, 150, 150, 1);
      }
      [data-text-editor-v1-${uniqueId}-plugin-styles='1'] .cm-content {
        line-height: normal;
        ${paddingTop ? `padding-top:${paddingTop}` : ""};
        ${paddingBottom ? `padding-bottom:${paddingBottom}` : ""};
      }
      [data-text-editor-v1-${uniqueId}-plugin-styles='1'] .cm-line {
        ${paddingLeft ? `padding-left:${paddingLeft}` : ""};
        ${paddingRight ? `padding-right:${paddingRight}` : ""};
      }
      [data-text-editor-v1-${uniqueId}-plugin-styles='1'] .cm-editor {
        height:100%;
        min-height:100%;
        max-height:100%;
        background-color: transparent !important;
        color: inherit !important;
      }
      [data-text-editor-v1-${uniqueId}-plugin-styles='1'] .cm-editor .cm-selectionBackground,
      [data-text-editor-v1-${uniqueId}-plugin-styles='1'] .cm-editor .cm-content ::selection {
        ${CSS.supports("background-color", "light-dark(blue, blue)") ? `background-color:light-dark(#d9d9d9, #3E4451) !important;` : ""}
      }
      [data-text-editor-v1-${uniqueId}-plugin-styles='1'] .cm-editor .cm-placeholder {
        pointer-events: none !important;
        user-select: none !important;
      }
      `;
    }
    
    let elementStylesObserver = new MutationObserver(mutations => { updateStyles(); });
    elementStylesObserver.observe(element, { attributes:true, attributeFilter:['style'] });

    // let lastElementRectHeight = null;
    // let elementResizeObserver = new ResizeObserver(entries => {
    //   updateCmEditorHeight();
    // });
    // elementResizeObserver.observe(element);

    updateStyles();
    setTimeout(updateStyles, 1);
    window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').addEventListener('change', e => {
      editorView.dispatch({effects: themeCompartment.reconfigure(e.matches ? darkTheme : lightTheme)});
      updateStyles();
    });

    editorView.dom.style.outline = "none";  
    
    element.view = editorView;
    // element.yDoc = yDoc;
    // element.yText = yText;
    // element.docId = docId;

    // Hackily triggers synchronous layout
    // EDIT: Commented out because it causes a *massive* (multi-second) initial render delay.
    // editorView.coordsAtPos(1);
    
    return element;
  }

  return createTextEditor(opts);

getCodemirror6Imports() =>

e(i,t.length+l.length));else{let t=i.length>>1;s.push(new e(i.slice(0,t)),new e(i.slice(t)))}}else s.push(l)}replace(t,s,o){if(!(o instanceof e))return super.replace(t,s,o);[t,s]=a(this,t,s);let l=n(this.text,n(o.text,r(this.text,0,t)),s),h=this.length+o.length-(s-t);return l.length<=32?new e(l,h):i.from(e.split(l,[]),h)}sliceString(t,e=this.length,i="\n"){[t,e]=a(this,t,e);let n="";for(let r=0,s=0;r<=e&&s<this.text.length;s++){let o=this.text[s],l=r+o.length;r>t&&s&&(n+=i),t<l&&e>r&&(n+=o.slice(Math.max(0,t-r),e-r)),r=l+1}return n}flatten(t){for(let e of this.text)t.push(e)}scanIdentical(){return 0}static split(t,i){let n=[],r=-1;for(let s of t)n.push(s),r+=s.length+1,32==n.length&&(i.push(new e(n,r)),n=[],r=-1);return r>-1&&i.push(new e(n,r)),i}}class i extends t{constructor(t,e){super(),this.children=t,this.length=e,this.lines=0;for(let e of t)this.lines+=e.lines}lineInner(t,e,i,n){for(let r=0;;r++){let
